x1a1(dkon brtsegs): ldan 'das shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyind pa yang gzhan ma lags/ sgyu ma nyid kyang gzhan ma lags te/ shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyind pa nyid kyang sgyu ma/ sgyu ma nyid kyang shes rab kyi pha rol tu
x1a2(dkon brtsegs): phyind pa'o// bcom ldan 'das nang stong pa nyid kyang gzhan ma lags/ sgyu ma yang gzhan ma lags te/ nang stong pa nyid kyang sgyu ma/ sgyu ma nyid kyang nang stong pa nyid do// bcom ldan 'das phyi stong pa nyid
x1a3(dkon brtsegs): kyang gzhan ma lags/ sgyu ma yang gzhan ma lags te/ phyi stong pa nyid kyang sgyu ma/ sgyu ma nyid kyang phyi stong pa nyid do// phyi nang bcom ldan 'das phyi nang stong pa nyid kyang gzhan ma lags/ sgyu ma yang
x1a4(dkon brtsegs): gzhan ma lags te/ phyi nang stong pa nyid kyang sgyu ma/ sgyu ma yang / phyi nang stong pa nyid do// bcom ldan 'das stong pa nyid stong pa nyid kyang gzhan ma lags/ sgyu ma yang gzhan ma lags te/ 
x1a5(dkon brtsegs): stong pa nyid kyang sgyu ma/ sgyu ma nyid kyang stong pa nyid stong pa nyid do// bcom ldan 'das chen po stong pa nyid kyang gzhan ma lagasasgyu ma yang gzhan ma lags te/ chen po stong pa nyid kyang gzhan
x1a6(dkon brtsegs): sgyu ma/ sgyu ma nyid kyang chen po stong pa nyid do// bcom ldan 'das don dam pa stong pa nyid kyang gzhan ma lags/ sgyu ma yang gzhan ma lags te/ don dam pa stong pa nyid kyang sgyu ma/ sgyu ma nyid
x1a7(dkon brtsegs): don dam pa stong pa nyid do// bcom ldan 'das 'dus byas stong pa nyid kyang gzhan ma lags/ sgyu ma yang gzhan ma lags/ 'dus byas stong pa nyid kyang gzhan sbrum/ sgyu ma nyid kyang 'dus
x1a8(dkon brtsegs): byas stong pa nyid do// bcom ldan 'das 'dus ma byas stong pa nyid kyang gzhan ma lags/ sgyu ma sa gzha 'dus ma byas stong pa nyid kyang sgyu ma/ sgyu ma nyid kyang 'dus ma byas stong pa nyid do// 
x1b1(dkon brtsegs): bcom ldan 'das mtha' las 'das pa stong pa nyid kyang gzhan ma lags/ sgyu ma nyid kyang gzhan ma lags te/ mtha' las 'das pa stong pa nyid kyang sgyu ma/ sgyu ma nyid kyang mtha' las 'das 'das pa
x1b2(dkon brtsegs): stong pa nyid do// bcom ldan 'das thog ma dang tha ma myed pa stong pa nyid kyang gzhan ma lags/ sgyu ma yang gzhan ma lags te/ thog ma dang tha ma myed pa stong pa nyid kyang sgyu ma/ sgyu ma nyid kyang thog
x1b3(dkon brtsegs): ma dang tha ma myed pa stong pa nyid do// bcom ldan 'das dor ba myed pa stong pa nyid kyang gzhan ma lags/ sgyu ma 'ang gzhanas la dang byed pa stong pa nyid kyang sgyu ma/ sgyu ma nyid kyang dor ba myed pa stong nyid do// 
x1b4(dkon brtsegs): bcom ldan 'das rang bzhin stong pa nyid kyang gzhan ma lagasarang bzhin stong pa nyid kyang sgyu ma/ sgyu ma nyid kyang rang bzhin stong pa nyid do// bcom ldan 'das chos thams cad stong pa nyid

x1b6(dkon brtsegs): gi mtshan nyid stong pa nyid gzhan ma lags ma lags sgyu ma nyid kyi rang gi mtshan nyid stong pa nyid sgyu ma/ sgyu ma nyid kyang rang gi mtshan pa nyid do// bcom ldan 'das myi dmyigs pa stong pa nyid kyang
x1b7(dkon brtsegs): smra gnan su phyo nga sgyu nga / das po spyad pa ban
x1b8(dkon brtsegs): ma lags/ sgyu ma yang gzhan ma lags te/ dngos po myed pa stong pa nyid kyang sgyu ma/ sgyu ma nyid kyang dngos po myed pa stong pa nyid do// bcom ldan 'das dngos po myed pa'i ngo bo nyid kyang gzhan ma lags/ 
x2a1(dkon brtsegs): bar de mi dmigs pa'i tshul gyis chos bstan to// tshor ba dben zhes bya bar de mi dmigs pa'i tshul gyis chos bstan to// 'du shes ma rtag ces bya bar de/
